1b1(rnying rgyud): na dunan su na na na
1b2(rnying rgyud): tan gyi chud ces d+hug/ ldan gyis grub pa'i sangs rgyas dkyil pa che po pa'i tshogs rnams ma tshig 'tshal lo// 'di ska bdag gis zlos pa'i rnam gcig na/
1b3(rnying rgyud): m+b+ha ldan 'dis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sdug srung thugs rdo rje'i bdag nyid yon tan rten las ma lus pa'i bdag po da nA~M/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams
1b4(rnying rgyud): rje ca mo'i nyag la du sa gas sa 'du 'phrul med patshan pa bzhugs so/ de du las brjod kyis mi ltung ba'i 'khong gyi zangs dang brgyas nas bzhugs pa ni/
1b5(rnying rgyud): bdeg shegs pa brgya ma dang / rnarjel kham rgya ma dang / rin pa tsa'i khamabyam dang / bsgye lamargya ma dang / las kyi la
2a1(rnying rgyud): tum dang / gas ma pa dang / khyim rgya mthu' 'a'amamatshan mjug dang / gzhan mong mong banub sgrolatshon pa brgya dang bcas pani 'dos te// brgyad mdzad
2a2(rnying rgyud): rgyu thal dag/ u ca / rnam chog na pa rgya zhi' du/ na nga/ pa seM 'i ngas rgya ma pa
2a3(rnying rgyud): drang / grub par gdon mi za ba'i long brgya ba sbrel dang / lam gyi long ba rgyab spel dang / rigs bzhi'i rgyal ba las long brgya ba phral gnyis gnyis su sprul pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams dpa' bo'i cha lpags
2a4(rnying rgyud): gyis 'gro ba 'dul ba dang / gzhan yang dbus long 'khor ba drug cu dang bcas pa ni 'di lta ste/ bde gshegs rdo rje'i rigs kyi dmus long ban+d+ha lA dang / bde gshegs rin chen rigs kyi dmub long
2a5(rnying rgyud): bdag shegs rlos kyi dkyis sang 'dug ga sa kyi gas kya ma rigs pa 'i bya rgyabasams dpa mas dpa pa'i
2b1(rnying rgyud): sems can kyad na mdzad pa dang / gzhan ma nga byed dang gyi rgya kyang la pa shas phul ba'i tho sa pakor rnams dang / gzhan dang na kya pa nams nang danan/ na nga nang na ga dugabatshogs pa dang gcig ngas
2b2(rnying rgyud): rnam par thar pa brgyad dang ldan pa'i phyir na mgo brgyad lag brgyad nang brgyad pa dang / ye shes drug dang ldan pa'i cing namago drug la gadrug nang drug pa da / phrug sung thags dang ldan pa phyir rnamag gsum lag gsupa dang gas
2b3(rnying rgyud): dang / gzhan yang sprul ba'i me 'phrug dang / rlung 'brug dang / yang sbal ba se'i byan lag dmar po dang bcas pa rnams ni/ rje btsun ma pa thAg ni ldan ma'i mkha' bde chen po las 'gro ba'i don du hral nas bzhugs so//
2b4(rnying rgyud): de nas sum pa blag gi la rnams ni na'i klu 'dis rnam par bgyul to// don dam chos nyid smras pa med palas/ rig dad ma rig kyu ma'i khyad par gyis/ rig pa'i 'byung ga nis 'khor ba kya na // las kyi dpe gzugs pa khamasu gas
2b5(rnying rgyud): gnas// dbang chen che mchog khyad par bstan pa'i phyir// dregs pa thams cad dbang du bsdu nas ni// sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung ba'i bus la bab// mi rtog chos kyi sgra las phyag rgyur ba zhes// zhes bskul lo// de nas bcom ldan
2b6(rnying rgyud): 'das pad+ma dbang chen nyid su skye ba med pa nam mkha' lte bu'i ngang nas/ gzugs su ye sh+yes lha ma'i skur bzhengs te/ sngags kyi rgyal po 'di nyid kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje las byung ngo // oM pad+ma ma hA shrI he ru ka sarba duSh+TA na ta ka ha na da ha btsa tre sarba/
2b7(rnying rgyud): gsung sngags su// oM badz+ra hrI dru sbyin Ta/ gsung gi sngags so// oM Ta ng+yas rdzu/ e Ar mdzem/ thugs kyi sngags so// yopa tu hU~M hi trag te ta dra drug ga rje rje tre+e lan kyang bzhin du/ yon te
3a1(rnying rgyud): so// oM hri tha badz+ra ts+tsha kr-ita de mad riSh+TeHha ya kI wa e ka dza Ti tsu lu hu lud+d+hi hrIHdzadzaH/ phrin las kyi sngags so// gsang sngags rnam pa lnga brjod pas/ 'jig rten khams rnams g.yo 'bral ldan
3a2(rnying rgyud): rdegs pa can rnams nyid 'dzag pas// dbang can pa la thabs skyed nga// rang thi ga rnams pa ste/ ma ma ma la cang gnas/ sralan pa can dums byangasate// sangs rgyas bstan pa sa //
3a3(rnying rgyud): bcas so// de nas 'khor la rab gzigs nas// lta ba dang ni spyod pa dang // dbyung gi dkyil 'khor dam tshig dang // sgrub dang phrin las rab bshad bya// snod kyi 'jig rten chos kyi dbyings// 'gyur ba med pas chos kyi dbyings// thugs
3a4(rnying rgyud): rje rgyun chad med pas dbyings// nyes pa'i skyon rnams bral bas dbyings// phrin las thogs pa med pas dbyings// chos rnams 'byung khungs gyur pas dbyings// bcud kyi sems can ye shes su// kun gzhi 'gyur med chos kyi sku// yid
3a5(rnying rgyud): ni rang byung ye shes sra// nyon mongs lnga rnams longs spyod rdzogs// blo lnga cing snang sprul pa'i sku// tshogs brgyad su gsum lhun gyis grub// zhe sdang dmyal ba'i 'jig rten 'di// 'gyur med rdo rje mo long gsal// ser sngas chags pa
3a6(rnying rgyud): dwags gnas// mnyam nyid ye shes rin chen 'byung // gti mug byol song lam gnas pa// chos dbyings rtag pa rnam snang mdzad// 'dod chags mi ste bde bar spyod// so sor kun rtog snang mtha' yas// nga rgyal lha dang lha ma yin//
3a7(rnying rgyud): bye ba nan tan don yod grub// rigs lngar rtogs pa 'di kun kyang // 'gro ba drug la rang bzhin gnas// 'gro drug gzugs su snang ba kun// pad+ma dbang chen nga yi sku// lha yi srog ni a dkar po// ri rab rtse gnas rol mo spyod// lha min su
3b1(rnying rgyud): ser sreg ldan pa// ni rag khong seng gnas nas 'khrugs// gling bzhir mi gnas ldang kun// byinang 'dod yon las la chags// rgyal song dung kha dra mtshogs// d+h+we rtsa mtsha nang na gnas// m-i dwags phre rab kres kyi zhom// rmong
3b2(rnying rgyud): khyer se skya'i gnas na spyod// dmyal ba'i rje nag cha grang can// rdo rje gdan 'og gnas pa yang // 'gro drug srog las gsung du 'byung // de yang dbang chen nga yi gsung // rigs drug sems kyi rang yang / da yin
3b3(rnying rgyud): khams tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi rnams// bsam gtan tha ba ni yo du banas// gzugs med kyi mched na bzhi AH// khams gsum lus dang ngag yid rnams// dang rkyen dru gcung thugs kyi gnas// na ci/
3b4(rnying rgyud): gnyis su med par bsdu bya'o// dpal pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi rgyud las gleng gzhi dang gleng bslang ba dang / dregs pa dbang du bsdus ning gsang ba'i sngags dang chos nyid yang dag pa'i su dgongs bstan pa'i le'u sde dang po'o//
3b5(rnying rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das pad+ma dbang chen 'khor 'das kyi bdag po chen po de la dor ba'i ting nge 'dzin la zhugs nas 'ji ga ces gsungs so// nal babyor tha ma bstan pa'i tshe// brtson 'grus rtsen po'i spong bas byung // 'dod pa'i longs spyod lnga rnams
3b6(rnying rgyud): chags med gus pa'i spyod pa smos// / zlu ma mnyes par tir da // srog skyes srog dang rgyang mad // rbadang tha mo ma la sogs// rdo slob dadon tham la// sras dang / yid gsum mnyes yon 'bral// chags med bang par spong nga/
3b7(rnying rgyud): rnal 'byor rje lding mnyan pa sam gyi// srog nyal ba mar spyad pa spyad// khasku brtson srang mnyan par brtson// gzhog ral gyon dong bsam pas 'bad// zhabs rngas bkan la yang yang bsam// drug can btud ni dmi bzung // dug med nas rnam
4a1(rnying rgyud): sa// / gsang+gA zhing rnas ldan rnams pa zlag/ dgapa 'dod byung ba no nga dpazhamamam tha~M smrag smra// dad gas

4a3(rnying rgyud): bslab// bas mag tan mnyam par 'jug pa tshe// til bus sgron ma lta bur snar// rjes gcod rnam bzhi mar dang dus// rgyun chad med par rgya bo bzhin// gzung bzhin mthar pa'i spyod pas
4a4(rnying rgyud): sems nyid lha dang bral miH// rnal 'byor gsang sngags zas pa'i dus// la bu ma yin snang ba min// chung na me sbyin grangs nas// byang brngamar brtag pa bzhin// ti ga tus gang bdeng na ces//
4a5(rnying rgyud): ba lan/ maman thar ba bas pa gyur/ dengs bub rna pa che na thogs sbyin nga ste// dgal ga' mar bar gyur bya// dam 'dzid dam chag nyal pa dang / nam pa thogs pa/ ya da gang ba
4a6(rnying rgyud): dpe// blon me dang de ldan pa dang // dug dang ldan dang chu pa 'i// na drA tshaM dang ngam ldan bzhin// dmachog nyams dang grags ma ci// la me rar+tha la zhwas grang pa mis// zab can ma smras dang bar spyong// spong ba 'di
4a7(rnying rgyud): byang cu ga ces par rab cu 'ad// skyen sa sa byer myod pa mas// zhing tu mi lus rnal bar bya// mthung ba'i myong ba yis// gzungs ma mtshan ldanas gyung ba// / sIr 'thong par 'o// 'a
4b1(rnying rgyud): bskyang bar bya// glang mkhan gzung spyod pa las// 'as pas sor mthun par gdul// ming tha~Mng ga zung spong pa yis// dadza mtshad lam babyung bar bya// dpa' ba su rgya snad pa las// bar cad dgra bgags gzhom par bya/
4b2(rnying rgyud): sngon rje sa bu pyod pa yis// rtsa ba yan lag dam chog bsrung // thun mo mdzangs pa'i spyod pa yis// dmadzes ma sras tshang ba bsags// rtag par byas ma thor rtsod pa dang // mngon po kun tu nupa dang // smad pa ma lus rnams cang ba
4b3(rnying rgyud): shes pa dus par zang ba sug pa bya'o// du nardzogs pa srung nag byed sa/ zas ngan mi dgasas kyi rnye pa bdun pa'i'i cu byeg ni/ de nas bamadan 'das byes
4b4(rnying rgyud): na la bye ba'i ched drugasangs sa// sems can pams thams cad / lus mi dbang na ni rdzogs pas na// dbang blani yang dag byin par n+tu/ da nang dang gas ba dang // mkhan ma bang cagasang // dbya
4b5(rnying rgyud): don bzlas so// sems cam khams ni ma sras pa'i// sras pa ma yi dkyil 'khor gnas// tham pa'i dbang med bathar ba ni// zam pa che brjod rgya yi dbang // sras kyi bag chags dag par byed// cang pan rin chen dbyung gnas
4b6(rnying rgyud): bdung bzhi'i tshogs lus rgyal bar byed// rdo rje snang ba mthang yas dbang // lhag zung 'tsho bdag bdud kyang 'joms// dris bu na ma 'grub pa'i dbang // chas rnams smra yang sgrogs par mdzad// gzugs grang rnam par sngar ma
4b7(rnying rgyud): de la du rje ming yang btags// dri de meng zas brgyad dbang baphre bas/ dra tha~Mng ba dag por yang dag drung// Shi T+wAM ga ni sa yasa?// shes rab Ta ma du ma sras// thabs dang shas rab gnyis meng par// ma dang ma
5a1(rnying rgyud): 'byud ba tudu gsal tha las dpang rnams can// bad bzlas s+ho/ pa'odas ga pa// dbas skyob padag dab pas sub / na

5a3(rnying rgyud): mya mtshan dang ldan pa la// lus kyi byor bas dal bus bsrub// ting 'dzin brtan pas nang du gzung // byang sems thig le mkhar 'bebs nas// rab ni ba dang be'u 'dra// 'bring ni byang ba me tog bzhin// thams pa dang bye'u ltar blangs

5a6(rnying rgyud): nas ni// bslab pas b+ha gar lizla bzhag/ rjes su dran pas bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas mnyes par mchod pa dang // sems can bde bas khyab par bya// bsgrub chen rdo rje pad+ma bsub// thig le dbang cing gzung bar bya// 'di

5b2(rnying rgyud): ge'i khog pa'ang // kye yis zhal kyi gdong yang khebs// sden mtshams mdzod spu bsgrub pa deng // dbu yi gtsug gtor brtan pa'i dus// thig le g.yas 'khyil dung gi gzugs// rang las hral ba'i zheng dmas na// 'a

5b4(rnying rgyud): na// lus dang ngag dang yid gsum gyi// dri ma ma lus dag pa yin// thams cad dag ces bya ba yang // dngos po gsal dag ma yin te// rgyud nas dag par byed pa yang // dper na sa bon btab pa la// dus su mang por gyur pa
5b5(rnying rgyud): ltar// dbang gi sa bon btab pa yis// rnal 'byor lus la lo tog srin// zhes gsungs so// pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi hud las/ dbang bskur ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan
5b6(rnying rgyud): 'das kyis dkyil 'khor 'di gsungs so// dkyil 'khor rab tu gang shes 'dod// snying po chos sku dri med dkyil// longs spyod rgyal ba rigs lnga 'khor// rang bzhin mthar phyin 'bras bu yin// snod kyi 'jig rten gzhal yas
5b7(rnying rgyud): khang // bcud kyi sems can lhar gnas par// rnal 'byor gang gis rtogs pa de// rang bzhin nyid kyi dkyil 'khor yin// rang bzhin dkyil 'khor chen po de// rtogs par mi ldan gang zag la// mtshon gying gzugs brtan
6a1(rnying rgyud): dkyil 'khor bstan// lugs pa bris skra 'brar dang thags// mkhas pas byas na sangs rgyas mthong // bde gshegs sgra bzhengs byin rlabs che// 'byor pa mi ldan gang zag la// dam tshan dkyil
6a2(rnying rgyud): 'khor chen po bstan// rab tu zlum po'i lte ba la// pad+ma gar gyi dbang phyug che// 'khor lo drug dang gru chad ldan// rtsibs drug kham rgya chen po drug/ bar khyam gnyis dang sgo bzhir bcas// dang po long ba dmas lo la/
6a3(rnying rgyud): gnyis par dpal gyi khyi brgyad dang // ye shes sprul pa'i khyi bcur gnas// sgo bzhir sgo srung bzhi rnams ni// mkhas pas bkod nas tha#// rta babs dur khrod rdor dang // me dmang 'bar bas rab tu 'khrigs// ya 'a thugs
6a4(rnying rgyud): da kyil 'khor ni// dbus su bad+ma gsang ba'i blo// hrI ni padz+ra nyi shu bzhi// zur bzhir ni chen khyi rkang ni// grwa chad bzhin rnam par gnas// bar khams dang bathong rus la// 'khor gyi long ba brgyad pa dang // dbus long drug
6a5(rnying rgyud): tu dgod pa yod// phyogs rer bco lnga bco lnga gnas// gnyis par me dpung khyi spyad la// sgo bzhi sgo ba rta babs dang // dur khrod me dpung 'bar bas 'khrigs// dkyil 'khor 'di ni gzi brjid can// nyi bla bzhin du gzir dang che
6a6(rnying rgyud): rnal 'byor spros pa sbyang nas gnas// ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor rab tu bsgom// brda dbang dman mgrin dbang // gang la mos pa rab tu bsam// bsus la dga' ba'i rnal 'byor bas// brgyad par chen sku gcig pa// dbu ma phyag
6a7(rnying rgyud): bcu drug pa// zhabs brgyad pa ni bsgom par bya// yang na blo chung mos pa can// rta mgrin g.yas dkar g.yon rdzob// dbus ma pad+ma rA ga'i sku// rdo rje kha T+wAM sbrul zhags g.yas// dril bu dung dmar lcags sgrog g.yon/
6b1(rnying rgyud): pad+ma ral gri yum la 'khril// 'di ltar bsgom par byed pa de// sangs rgyas thob par gdon mi za// rnam par smin pa'i rig 'dzin ni// rang sems lha skur nang du smin// bag chags lus ni phyin gsal// brkos phor nang gi snga tshwa 'dra// yul
6b2(rnying rgyud): ni sangs rgyas gdul zhing ste// bla ma dam pas 'dul bar mdzad// tshe la dbang ba'i rig 'dzin ni// rang don lo ni stong dang ni// drug brkyar rang gi don du bzhugs// gzhan gyi don du bzhugs 'dod na// gyis pa lo brgyad lon tsam du// brgya bcu dag tu bskur
6b3(rnying rgyud): zhing gnas// pad+ma dag la brdzus nas phye// lha mi'i lus ni khyad par can// skye ba bzhes nas 'gro don mdzad// sprul pa sgra yi bla ma la// zhing khams kun tu dam chos nyan// phyag rgya chen po'i rig 'dzin ni// rang lus sangs rgyas bsgom 'dzin pa//
6b4(rnying rgyud): longs spyod rdzogs su rigs lnga'i 'khor// rgyal ba rnams las chos kyang nyan// shar na mngon par dga' ba'i zhing // rdo rje sems dpa'i sras su 'khrungs// lhon dpal dang ldan pa ste// rin chen 'byung ldan 'khor na gnas// nub na bde ba chen po
6b5(rnying rgyud): na// snang mtha' yas la chos kyang nyan// byang na rnam dag bkod pa ru// don yod grub pa'i rigs su phye// dbus phyogs byang chub snying po ru// rnam par snang mdzad zhal mthong nas// phyag rgya chen po'i rig 'dzin nyid// rang lus lha lur smin pa'o//
6b6(rnying rgyud): sman gyis grub pa'i rig 'dzin ni// mnyam par gzhag tshe chos kyi sku// langs tshe longs spyod rdzogs lus thob// zhing khams nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam// rgyan dang gdan dang 'od zer sogs// sangs rgyas che ba'i yon tan thob// ces gsungs
6b7(rnying rgyud): pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi rgyud las/ dkyil 'khor gyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dam tshig 'di dag gsungs so// shel sgong dkar po dri med 'di// 'dam du nam yang bying mi bya// yid
7a1(rnying rgyud): bzhin nor du re skong ba// ma rnyed par du btsal bar bya// chu bo rab med grol mkhan la// drin ni nams kyang bkur bar bya// rin chen gser gyi sbom bral// zhabs su bug pa ba ra \u0f7f// pa yi dang nga
7a2(rnying rgyud): lcags chen po// 'tshogs kyang bsrang bar mi bya'o// me tog u dum war la// lag gis brtse bar mi bya'o// tsan+dan smug po'i sdong po la// bud shing bya ba'i sems mi gtong // lcags kyi thu lum 'bar ba la// lag pas gzung 'ar mi n+ya
7a3(rnying rgyud): gser gyi ri la 'bab pa'i chu// nams kyang btung bar mi bya'o// seng ge dkar mo'i nyal shul du// mal ni bca' bar mi bya'o// rgya mtsho chen po'i 'jing chu la// gru ni sad par mi bya'o// rin po che yi za ma tog/ dug gis skur bar mi bya'o//
7a4(rnying rgyud): par dam tshig bcu gnyis 'di// rnal 'byor dam la gnas pa yis// rang gi srog bzhin rtag tu bsrung // ma bsrungs nyams pa'i chad pas 'phog/ rdo rje dmyal bar ltung bar 'gyur// bsrungs na yon tan bsam mi khyab// mchog dang thu mong dngos
7a5(rnying rgyud): grub 'thob// ces gsungs so// pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi rgyud las/ sa gzhi rin po che lta bu'i dam tshig bstan pa'i le'u lnga pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bsgrub pa rnam par bkod pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyems par zhugs/
7a6(rnying rgyud): nas 'di gsungs so// bsgrub pa'i don yang gnyis yod de// mchog gi bsgrub pa bya ba dang // thun mong dngos grub bsgrub pa'o// mchog gi bsgrub pa rnam pa gnyis// bskyed pa'i rim pa bsgom pa dang // rdzogs pa'i rim pa bzang po bgom// bskyed
7a7(rnying rgyud): pa'i rim pa bsgom bya ba// sku gsung thugs rje'i 'byung tshul gyis// ting 'dzin rnam gsum bsgom par bya// yul nyid sangs rgyas zhing khams yin// 'byung ba rim brtsegs steng du ni// dbang chen gzhal yas khang yang bsgom// rin chen khri rkang
7b1(rnying rgyud): seng ge dang // pad+ma nyi bla'i gdan steng du// gar gyi dbang phyug chen po bsam// dbu lnga dmar po gshog pa bzhi// phyag ni bcu drug zhabs brgyad pa// sku la bkod pa'i dkyil 'khor dgra// 'khor ni kham rgya chen mo drug/ long ba brgyad dang de yi 'khor/
7b2(rnying rgyud): dbus long drug cu lcags sbyang brgyad// ye shes sprul pa'i khyi bcu dang // slob bzhi dang me rlung 'phrug/ yang sprul bsaM yi byan lag rnams// rim par bskyed nas brten par dmigs// de nas spyan drang bzhugs su gsol// phyag dang mchod
7b3(rnying rgyud): pas mnyes par bya// de nas bzlas brjod bsnyen pa dbul// bstod cing bshags nas phrin las bcol// dam tshig bsdus la ye shes gshegs// spyod lam kun tu lha nyid bsam// phyi rabs sngags 'chang sgrub pa la// ngas ni khyod la
7b4(rnying rgyud): gsal bar bshad// rdzogs rim bsgom pa'i rnal 'byor pas// gang zag gzer dang sgom thabs dang // 'bras bu bzhi ni dpa' bos bshad// brtson 'grus can dang le lo can// brtson 'grus can gyi gang zag ni// tshe 'dir mngon par 'tshang rgya bar
7b5(rnying rgyud): yan lag rnam pa brgyad ldan dgos// rgyal nus pa thogs med pas// sngon nas bsod nams bsags pa dang // rigs kyang khyad par can du 'khrungs// longs spyod 'byor pa che ba dang // gtor phod tshe dang tshe ring ba// brtson 'grus che zhing dad pa che// de
7b6(rnying rgyud): brgyad ldan pa'i gang zag la// brtson 'grus can gyi gang zag skye// bsgyur ba bdun gyi sangs rgyas te// sngags kyis skur yang bsgyur ba dang // rang lus byin gyis rlobs pa dang // ngag kyang byin gyis rlobs pa dang // sems nyid byin gyis rlobs pa dang //
7b7(rnying rgyud): kun rdzob bde chen byin gyis rmobs// 'od gsal bar ni byin gyis rlobs// zung du 'dug par byin rlobs so// le lo can gyi gang zag de// srid pa bar dor 'tshang rgya bas// yan lag bdun dang man ngag gnyis// yan lag bdun dang ldan par

8b1(rnying rgyud): skyes na// nal 'byor lam drang sa bya// sems kyang ba mos sgrar gcig/ smyon dbang pa nam yar 'byung // thu sul thar ba rnas pa gnyis// rang ba gtus dang me snang gnyis// 'thal bung byung ba'i thang ngan// 'ams da /
8b2(rnying rgyud): grong khyer gsum du snang // ma 'khrul pa yi snang ba ni// sems nyid 'di gsal rang bzhin nyid// mi snang ba la gnyis yod de// 'grel pa dag gis mi sbyar ba// ri bong de dang mo gsham za// nam mkha'i me tog rus thal gru// seng ge'i
8b3(rnying rgyud): sogs pa// mi srid pa yi chos rnams yin// ma 'khrul pa yi snang ba ni// 'dus ma byas pa'i chos nyid ni// nam mkhar 'dzin pa dang bral ba// chos su dri ma med pa'o// sems can rnams kyi thog gyur pa// chung zhes bya bas las
8b4(rnying rgyud): kun byed// 'di ni rnam shes bzhon rta ste// lnga yi bdag nyid bcu ming can// rang bzhin phra ba brgya dang ni// drug nu them pa 'di dag ni// rlung gi bzhon pa'i rgyu yin te// nyin dang mtshan du rgyu ba yi// de yang ji ltar rab rgyu ba// srog 'a
8b5(rnying rgyud): ni srog gyur pas// sems dang tha dad med par gcig/ rtogs dang ma rtogs khyad par gyis// 'khor 'das kun gyi las byed de// rlung rnams kun gzhi nyon mongs dang // yid dang sgo lnga snang ba ni// rlung rnams phra ba'i gzugs kyis ni//
8b6(rnying rgyud): shes dang yang dag 'dres gyur nas// dbang po'i lam las byung nas ni// yul rnams kun la 'jug par 'gyur// rtsa ba'i phung po'i rlung lnga ni// srog 'dzin me mnyam khyab par byed// gyen dang thur du rgyu bar 'dod// yan lag dbang po'i rlung
8b7(rnying rgyud): lnga ni// mig la mi yi rlung rgyu bas/ gzugs rnams thams cad mthong bar byed// rna bar rlung gi rlung rgyu bas// skra rnams thams cad thos par byed// rna la sa yi rlung rgyu bas// dri rnams ma lus tshor bar byed// kyel chu yi chung
9a1(rnying rgyud): rtsa/ rgyabs// ro rnams thams cad myong bar byed// lus la nam mkha'i nang rgyubs// reg bya ma lus nyams su myong // rmyi dang nang gartog pa rnams// rtsal chung zhon nu bar byed// rang bzhin rtog bcas brdung /
9a2(rnying rgyud): bu nyid// rlung gi bzhon rtas nyin mtshan rgyu// de phyir chung zin bsgom par 'gyur// ril por 'dzin pa'i rnam pa ni// mgo bo nas ni rkang pa'i bar// ji srid snying gar phyin gyi bar// rnal 'byor yang dag mtha' la 'dug/ ril por 'dzin pa zhes
9a3(rnying rgyud): bshad do// de bzhin rjes su gzhig pa ni// ji ltar dbugs kyi me long la// mtha' nas rim gyi dbus khyim ltar// rnab 'byor yang dag mtha' la 'jung // rjes su gzhig pa zhes bshad do// sems de kun tu ldang ba ni// mas la
9a4(rnying rgyud): so sor spyod// rang bzhin kun tu snang ba ni// yid kyi rnam shes ma g.yos pa'o// mtshan bcas bsgom pa 'di ltar bya// mtshan bcas nyid du bsgom pa dang // mtshan bcas mtshan ma med par bsgyur// mtshan bcas 'byung ba'i cho ga dang // byang
9a5(rnying rgyud): nas brtan par bya ba'o// mtshan bcas 'byung ba'i cho ga ni// bltas pas spang bar bya ba dang // ma bslad pa yi gang zag la// sems gzung la sogs bltas pas 'ong // bsgom pas spang bar bya ba yang // ma bslang gang zag bsgom dgos
9a6(rnying rgyud): pas// glo bur sgra la blta zhing bsgom// bshur bas 'ong bar bya ba ni// ji ltar sprin ni sna tshogs pa// mdog dang dbyibs ni tha dad pas// nam mkha'i ngang las byung nas ni// de nyid du ni thim par 'gyur// de bzhin rang bzhin thams
9a7(rnying rgyud): cad kun// don ni brgyad cu de la yang // 'dod chags rtog pa bzhi badz+ra dang // zhe sdang sum cu rtsa gsum dang // gti mug rtog pa bdun sogs pa// snang ba gsum gyi rgyu can te// mi lus yul la gzhug nas ni// 'od gsal bar ni

10a2(rnying rgyud): mtshan pa lha sgral dga' na// brtan pa'i cho ga byas la ni// mdo tsam bsgom dang ris mi bsgom// mi gsal na yang de ltar bsgom// sems ni 'phro ba dgag par bya// gnyis su med pa'i spyod pa bya// spos bcas dang ni glos med da
10a3(rnying rgyud): shin tu spos med spyod pa bya// mtshan ma la ni nan tan brtag/ de la mtshan med shugs kyis 'char// rnam par grol ba'i lam de ni// de kho na nyid man ngag dang // de dang rjes mthun spyod pa'o// mtshan ma med la man ngag gnyis//
10a4(rnying rgyud): dgra bsal lam nyid bsgom// de la bar chod dgrar yang bzhi// dgra 'dul ba yi man ngag dang // dgra de btson du bzung ba dang // dgra ni tshar yang gcad pa dang // dgra la dgrar mi 'dzin pa yin// dgra 'dul ba ni be shur nga gnyis//
10a5(rnying rgyud): dus // sa /

10a7(rnying rgyud): dgra bo btson bzung spyod pa gnyis// phyi dang nang gi spyod pa'o// gyi'i spyod sgo lnga'i rnam shes ni// yul la mi gtang dang lugs 'jug/ nang gi spyod pa sems mi 'phro// dgra de tshar yang gcod par bya// mi dmigs pa yis dus dang ni// 'o dgas
10b1(rnying rgyud): sa dgra bsas// dpal dbar ma dzin pa// gzugs sa ga rnam par slab ste// rtswa yang dgang ma ngan dug/ zang 'ab pa'is na// 'am dang can du rung bags// banyam par ma dazhug dus dum
10b2(rnying rgyud): dbang dzin gnyis// mnyam par gzhig pa'i dus na'o// pas nyid rnam pa'i margyan med pani// gnas pa dang na ma dmigs pa// 'dags pa kyang du 'jug pa'o// gnas pa sa mas ni bzur bar bya// bzur ba med du tsaman/
10b3(rnying rgyud): sems ni rang log nyid du gyur// bshur ba tshad du phyin pa yin// lal tshang du phyin pas 'thob// la la bden pa'i sgo nas 'thob// la la shes pa 'tshams pas 'thob// la la kha bo dag gis thob// la lar spros pa bcad pas thong // de dang
10b4(rnying rgyud): mthun byed pa gsum// gos bcas spyod pa mtshan mar spod// spos mod sdod pa gsang pyod de// shin tu zlos med spyod pa yin// bus pa rnams la ma bstan te// nus pa med pas gyod mi nus// rgang po rnams pa ma bstan te// nas
10b5(rnying rgyud): byi na nus pa shor// nal 'byor min la mi bstan to// le lo rkyen gyi spyod yul min// shin tu spros med ma mongs pa// nal 'byor pA la bstan pa yin// bsgom pa thams cad de las byung // lta ba bsgom du med pa ni// spong ba yongs su mer
10b6(rnying rgyud): pa yin// mtshan ma med pa'i man ga yid// de na gnyis med pasgom par bya// gnyis med pa nom pa'i tu la ni// dang mor sems ni gnas pa bya// de nas sems ni dmigs pa ste// dmigs pa skyes pa'i tid lani// rang bzhin gyis ni 'ong

11a1(rnying rgyud): ba dan dam bdan pa las// rtsub ma lus kun rdzog yin// byas pa zlang 'jug dpar mad// das na kyis 'cha ba yang // srung ba khams dang byamachad rnams// 'byung bldan pa bzhal zin/
11a2(rnying rgyud): 'byung ba chen po bzhi po yang // swa ni rtsal thim par 'gyur// chu ni me la bim par 'gyur// me ni chung la brim par 'gyur// rgyung ni rnam par shes la bim// rnam shes snang ba de la thim// snang ba snang ba mched la brim// snang mched sdang ba
11a3(rnying rgyud): thob la thim// snang ba thob pa bya ba ni// thams cad stong pa nyid la thim// der ni yongs rdzogs rnal 'byor gyis// gsol ba'i don ni bshad bya ste// stod pa gsum po rnam dag gang // 'od gsal ba ni 'di bshad do// bsam gtan 'di ni
11a4(rnying rgyud): bsam gtan min// 'dis ni mthar thug mi thob ste// nam mkha' lta bur gyogs gyur pas// 'od gsal ba ni 'di dmigs shing // 'od gsal ba ni gnas thob pas// rab dga' gzugs su skye bar 'gyur// de tsho ba dag 'ardo rje'i chu/
11a5(rnying rgyud): kun gyi dbang phyug thob par 'gyur// 'das pa dang ni ma 'ongs pa// da ltan du ba'i srid pa gsum// 'od gsal ba ni rnam dag pas// skad cig gcig lam lus mthong // thams cad stong pa 'od gsal ba// shing shes rab rol gyid// dang
11a6(rnying rgyud): bar gshegs pa'i snying po yin// rnal 'byor pa yi grogs yin no// de las chos bu 'byung ba ni// par ma da~M li su yin te// ji ltar chu chung dengs pa las// nya dag myur du 'phar ba ltar// de bzhin thams cad sbyong gsal las// rgyu 'drang ni 'byung
11a7(rnying rgyud): bar bshad// sngon 'byung srid pa'i sha gzugs can// dbang po kun tshang thogs med ldan// rigs mthun lha mig dag pas mthong // bar mdo yi bu de yin// 'gro ba rigs drug grong khyer te// gnyis su med pa'i spyod pas bcad// smos pa'i
11b1(rnying rgyud): rnam zang gyur nas// byang ma do yi srud ni// rdo rje sems dpa'i spun bsgom// mo 'di nyid kyis thams cad mthen// sangs rgyas zhing nas mi ldog pas// bar mA da du mngon 'chang na// 'dra gsal ba ni brnam par bya// zung 'jug phra yang 'thung dudu
11b2(rnying rgyud): 'gyur// kun rdzob dang ni don dam dge/ so so'i cha yis phye gyur no// yang dag nyid du 'dres gyur pas// zung du 'jug par de bshad do// zung du 'jug pa gnyis yod de// slob bzhin pa dang mi slob pa// mi slob pa ru gyur tsam na// bar
11b3(rnying rgyud): mdo ru mngon sangs rgya// snang ba tsam dang gsal btsam// snang la rang gzhon med pa gnyis// sangs rgyas zhing nas mi ldog pas// bar ma do ru mngon sangs rgya// 'bras bu bu gsum thob 'gyur ba// chos su dri ma med pa dang // longs su rgyal
11b4(rnying rgyud): rigs lnga dang // sbrul gru mdzad pa mthar phyin zhus// bdag gzhan ma lus bsrung ba dang // 'gegs dang bar chad bzlog pas na// bdag don bregs pa srung bzlog yin// zhes gsungs so// pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi rgyud las/ mchog
11b5(rnying rgyud): gi dngos grub bsgrub pa ste le'u drug pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das dpal pad+ma dbang chen gyis thun mong gi dngos grub bdag gzhan gyi bar tshod srung bzlog 'di gsungs so// gti mug gru gnyenas bdag dang // 'dod chags ma
11b6(rnying rgyud): bdud mo dang // zhe sdang gshin rje la sogs pa'i// rang gi bar chod srung ba dang // phas kyi grong ba bzlog par gsungs// oM a g+ho te ka yA mar+d+ha ka e sa ra hU~M phaT/ e te pre te yas nan mra twod kar k+Sha rak+Sha/ pho rgyad thams cad spang ba'i sngags so//
11b7(rnying rgyud): a i ni ba zhi dri shi dra ba ni de gi rung shi ki kyai n+yo// ta pa li mu li du ru ru hUM phaT/ kaM ma tsan+da mu ti d+ya r+ya hU~M phaT/ rakra mra te ru lu ru lu hU~M dz+yod+ha/ e kA R+tha nIts+tshi pA la mi sha dgra bo la phaT/ nag mo ri ma ti bdA mi ta ra ti ru ti ra ma ti ha rbad ts+tsha/ mo rgyud thams cad srung ba'i sngags so//
12a1(rnying rgyud): nag ma thas/ g+sa sa// sa sa chags / klu na/
12a2(rnying rgyud): yan rlung 'grod/ ya~M te byar thag khrol ba yang du brjo/ sa ma ya su ma thing rlob/ de rgyud thams cadadang rlog pa'i sngags so// a tsa dur ma ma sbyong na brjod/ mamo tsar ya zlog/ stan thag ga mo cheng / datha ma te sha na sre to// gcon
12a3(rnying rgyud): ya klo \u0f7f/ mo cud thams cad bklog pa'i sngags so// oM gA ru Ta tsa le tsa le sa nA gdun zlog ta ki tsa te bi te pu me ra tsa ba zlog/ hu ya pu ya sa khrag ra tsa ya klong/ hu lu hu lu nA gar cal thog/ su ru te sud+ya te sab+hA ga rAm pa badz+ra thams cad dil te
12a4(rnying rgyud): so/ de nas rang gshed dbab pa ni// gshin rje skyes pa'i lto bar bri// rabs chad thod pa'i nang du stsal// seng lde dpur pas gzir ba'i sngags/ ya ma thig nan/ ya bur thims dza/ mA ra ya rbad/ ma mo zhing gi pags sA la// bud med rto sa pa
12a5(rnying rgyud): snrel gre'athod pa'i nang du stsal/ seng ldeng phur pas gdab pa'i sngags/ ma ma ru lu dzi ga nan/ ma hu ra thams dza/ mA ra ya thar/ mu stegs bon po'i lto bar rje// mon thod nang du dug rgyas brdag tai ra ti ka tri ga nan/ dzakur thams dza/ bA ra ma zad// \u0f88\u0f90 ni
12a6(rnying rgyud): ldog pa'am// shing sdong nang du bri bar zla// mi dkar lto bar bris nas ni// mdzo tol thod pa'i nang du gzhug/ gtor mas brdeg par byas nas ni// shing gi phur bas gdab par bya/ de pa tri ga nan/ e hur thams rba/ mA ra yi rbad// radagar
12a7(rnying rgyud): bri ba yang // rin po srin mo'i gzugs bris nas// rabs chad thod par lcags kyis drag/ gri lcags phrar bas brdeg pa'i sngags/ rag tu rtsig nan/ ra hur thams dza/ mA ra ma rbad/ rig mo thig nan/ d+mar thams de/ mAr ya /
12b1(rnying rgyud): bzud po rtanag lto bar bya// g.yag zung su phul dud pas bdug/ byer bur thogs la sngags 'dis gzing / ru tra trig nan/ du phur zums rnga/ mA ra ya rbad/ bdud mo 'bri yi lto bar bris// dre'u thod krung kar dud pas bdug/ lcags pur thogs
12b2(rnying rgyud): la sngags 'dis gzir/ dun ting tri ga nan/ du hur thums dza/ mA ra ya rbad// gnod srin po mo gzir ba ni// kha nas me 'bar lto bar bris// mi tshil dung pas ta thong bdug/ mchog phur sngags 'dis gzir bar bya/ yak+Sha tri ga nan/
12b3(rnying rgyud): hur thums dza/ mA ra ya rbang / yag mo tri ga nan/ k+Sha hur thums dza/ mA ra ya rbad// btsan ni sha ba'i lto bar bris// mu zi'i dud pas 'khor lor bdug/ sha ru'i nang du lcags phur gzir/ yaM tri tri ga nan/ tsa hur thums dza/ mA ra ya
12b4(rnying rgyud): rbad// rgyal po ra dkar g.yang gzhir bris// byi ba'i thod par yunga? kar thun// lcags phur gzir ba'i sngags 'di'o// rA tsa tri gA nan/ tsa hur thums dza/ mA ra ya rbad/ dmu ni phug rod lto bar bri// rta nag thod par zangs phye'i thun/
12b5(rnying rgyud): bdug nas bri zhing brab pa'i sngags/ mu na mun tri ga nan/ sa hu ra zlums dza/ mA ra ya rbad/ rdo rje legs pa ra kham ltor// khyi nag thod par yung+ga kar bdug/ seng ldeng phur par sngags 'dis gzir/ badz+ra sA d+hU tri ga nan/ tri hur thums dza/
12b6(rnying rgyud): mA raM ya rbad/ rigs ngan pa na de'i lto bar bris/ mdze thod gtor zor ral gris brdeg/ ru tra tri ga nan/ nr-i hur thams dza/ mA ra ya rbad/ yul bdag lug nag lto bar bri// rabs chang thod par mtshon sna tshogs// kyi tshe thun brab sngags
12b7(rnying rgyud): 'dis gzir/ ro li thig nan/ trai Tar rnams dza/ mA ra ya zad/ 'gong po byas pa'i lho dar dri// bong bu'i thod par sre long thun/ ha shi tri ga nan/ ri nur thams dza/ mA ra ya rbad/ dam sre b+hi dmar lto bar bri// khyi thod nang du
13a1(rnying rgyud): mchog phur gzer// khyi dmar thun gyi thun gyis brag/ rba tri tri ga nan/ tri hur thams na/ mA rA ya rbad/ gruni tshangs pa'i spro bar bre// glang dmar nga nang gArtsis byugs// rtamig thun gyis 'ag
13a2(rnying rgyud): drug cig nan/ phrathar rnams pa/ mA ra sa tshang/ gtan na theg pa'i lte bar gyi/ TI dru thaM par mtshogs can/ pan+d+he thAgan/ zu mams pa/ sngar labang// bdi ga mas pa/ gzung
13a3(rnying rgyud): drig ste tshogs kyis thab par bya/ sa gadz+rag nan/ su hur thams / mAr ya tsang/ dregs pa kyi ma gzer ba ni// dA rgal yi sgo bar bri// da dog thod par spang lag zad// ram chen dkar glan pa me dang byas thA/ badz+ra
13a4(rnying rgyud): nan/ mi ci thams / slar sabang// gas bar parnams mtshugs na// gzugs rnams gang byang dris nas de// 'ams dus su gsum gzug/ gang pa gcigatu/ thar des gnyid nas das gang pa nga/
13a5(rnying rgyud): 'gal bsogs/ sarba duwAn ce/ zad na/ sarba tsan mo zad nan/ sha trUM mA ra yA rbad nan/ de nas rang ra gnas su mnan// thog dang ser ba dbab pa ni// dpral yaM lta bar gzer/ darje sarba tranan/ tsaH danan/ grom bram rjel trail shar
13a6(rnying rgyud): waM bri sa pa/ drag pos gzir ngo // badz+ras rba shAn rdeg nan/ bram zam thA la dzi la shar shAr b+hu phob/ rang bzhin gyis gzir ba ro// bajas pa na/ ba nan/ ma ba ga zad nan/ brim dzam dza la dz+wal ga sha su pang / nga zabs
13a7(rnying rgyud): gzor ba'o// sarba ben ci zad nan/ sarba du dz+nyAn tsonyi bdanan/ brom bro ma dzel dril shar shar sruba'o/ rdzogs pas gzir bar// sras ngan na tshogs gtsang bani// dzad par sras ngan rdza chags gzugs/ am mdu ng+yas gnal/ e tsa bran dang /
13b1(rnying rgyud): nan e dza thun pho ba/ hur thums dza/ mA ra ya rbad// ces gsungs so// pad+ma dbang chen dregs pa srung bzlog gi nA da las/ thun mong gi bsrub pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis phrin las 'di dag yongs su gsungs so//
13b2(rnying rgyud): te mug can gyi sems can la// zhe 'di las kyis gdul ba bya// chu cung chuba'i dus dag tu// pA'i tshogs kyi dkyil 'khoraH// dargya can 'byas pa'i las// sa su rgyu ba'i dus su ni// ma me tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor du// tshe dang bsod nams da
13b3(rnying rgyud): 'dod chags can la dbang gi las// me chung chu ba'i dus su bya// daM kyi tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor du// yul khams bud med rgyal po bsdu// zhe sdang can la drag po'i las// rlung gi drung chus g.yeng zhing 'jor// e yi tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor du//
13b4(rnying rgyud): bgegs pa lus bsgral paraH// phrin las bzhi yi dus dag tu// bdag nyid phyag rgya bzhi ldan bsgom// gtso ba phyag rgya chen po ste// spyan gyis grub pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgob// yul na ma chog phyag// yar ni don las mi 'da' bsgom// 'gro 'bul
13b5(rnying rgyud): kyi phyag rgya ste// mchod 'dul sgrib byang dngos grubazang // de dag ma lus cir snang yang // chos nyid dang las ma g.yos kyang // zhi ba chos nyid phyag rgya yin// 'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa'i chos// phyag rgya bzhi la 'phros shing 'dus// e waM ma yA'i yi ge bzhis//

300a2(rnying rgyud): 'khor lo// kA ya wA ka tsit+ta/ hUM hUM hUM/ hU~M hU~M hUM/ hUM hUM hUM/ rdo rje nyi ma nub nas ni// dngos grub chen po blang par bya// sman chen 'di yi bsod nams ni// lhag nyand ma sgong phrin las 'grub// rig 'dzin bzhi dang sgrub pa brgyad// he huka yi gsung bzhi nang // 'grub par 'gyur te gdon
300a3(rnying rgyud): gal te 'di la gzugs yod na// 'jig rten srog chags thams cad kyis// brjod par nus pa ma yin no// rdo rje bdud rtsi sman chen de// gsum du bgos la spyad par bya// mdor na mang po smos nyi dgos// bde gshegs thams cad mchod pa bas// 'di nyid bsgrub pa'i khyad par ni// lhag pa
300a4(rnying rgyud): bas kyang ches lhag go// 'di ma yin pa'i bsod nams ni// gzhan na nam yang yod ma yin// de bas bsgrub pa 'bad par bya// dpal he ru ka'i rgyud las/ rdo rje bdud rtsi bslab pa'i le'u ste dku pa'o// // de nas khrag 'thung chen po des/ de skad ces bka' stsal nas/
300a5(rnying rgyud): lha dang / srin po dang / gi nga dang / lang ka dang / ma bdun dang / srang mo bzhi dang / 'bar ma'i tshogs thams cad yi rangs te/ dgyes pa'i gad mo bsgrags te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bstod do// khrag 'thung rtsa ba'i rgyud thugs kyi gal po zhes bya ba
300a6(rnying rgyud): rdzogs so// / urgyan gyi mkhan po chen po pad+ma sa ma b+ha ba dang / lo tsA ba dge slong nam mkha'i snying pos bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// / nub phyogs u t+yan gyi gnas nas slob dpon hUM ka ras bton pa'o// rgyud 'di'i bka'i srung ma ni/
300a7(rnying rgyud): mkha' 'gro ma gtsug gi rgyan gcig ma dang srog gi nyul lem bzhi la gtad de// bka'i dus tshigs dang nyi tshod las 'das na mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis chad pa chod cig/ bka' rgya gsum mo//
